03997   /*
03998    *  This function searches the compressed table efficiently.
03999    */
04000   static unsigned long
04001   ft_get_adobe_glyph_index( const char*  name,
04002                             const char*  limit )
04003   {
04004     int                   c = 0;
04005     int                   count, min, max;
04006     const unsigned char*  p = ft_adobe_glyph_list;
04007 
04008 
04009     if ( name == 0 || name >= limit )
04010       goto NotFound;
04011 
04012     c     = *name++;
04013     count = p[1];
04014     p    += 2;
04015 
04016     min = 0;
04017     max = count;
04018 
04019     while ( min < max )
04020     {
04021       int                   mid = ( min + max ) >> 1;
04022       const unsigned char*  q   = p + mid * 2;
04023       int                   c2;
04024 
04025 
04026       q = ft_adobe_glyph_list + ( ( (int)q[0] << 8 ) | q[1] );
04027 
04028       c2 = q[0] & 127;
04029       if ( c2 == c )
04030       {
04031         p = q;
04032         goto Found;
04033       }
04034       if ( c2 < c )
04035         min = mid + 1;
04036       else
04037         max = mid;
04038     }
04039     goto NotFound;
04040 
04041   Found:
04042     for (;;)
04043     {
04044       /* assert (*p & 127) == c */
04045 
04046       if ( name >= limit )
04047       {
04048         if ( (p[0] & 128) == 0 &&
04049              (p[1] & 128) != 0 )
04050           return (unsigned long)( ( (int)p[2] << 8 ) | p[3] );
04051 
04052         goto NotFound;
04053       }
04054       c = *name++;
04055       if ( p[0] & 128 )
04056       {
04057         p++;
04058         if ( c != (p[0] & 127) )
04059           goto NotFound;
04060 
04061         continue;
04062       }
04063 
04064       p++;
04065       count = p[0] & 127;
04066       if ( p[0] & 128 )
04067         p += 2;
04068 
04069       p++;
04070 
04071       for ( ; count > 0; count--, p += 2 )
04072       {
04073         int                   offset = ( (int)p[0] << 8 ) | p[1];
04074         const unsigned char*  q      = ft_adobe_glyph_list + offset;
04075 
04076         if ( c == ( q[0] & 127 ) )
04077         {
04078           p = q;
04079           goto NextIter;
04080         }
04081       }
04082       goto NotFound;
04083 
04084     NextIter:
04085       ;
04086     }
04087 
04088   NotFound:
04089     return 0;
04090   }
04091 
04092 #endif /* FT_CONFIG_OPTION_ADOBE_GLYPH_LIST */
